***боеспособный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:боеспособный.html>боеспосо́бный</a> (29660)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">battle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:способный.html>спосо́бный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sposóbnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">capable, able</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kampffähig</i>. First attested in 1887 [see citations]
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боеспособный.html>боеспосо́бный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bojesposóbnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)боеспосо́бнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)боеспосо́бней</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">боеспосо́бнейший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>battleworthy</li></ol>

***божий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:божий.html>бо́жий</a> (2965)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">box</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:божий.html>бо́жий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bóžij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>God's, divine</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:божок.html>божо́к</a> (24966)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">box</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:божок.html>божо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">božók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:божок.html>божка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:божок.html>божки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:божок.html>божко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">box</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (a little) god</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> idol, someone loved by the public</li>
<li>a figurine or a small statue of a god</li></ol>

***бой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a> (672)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bojь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰoyh₂ós</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰeyh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to strike, hew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to beat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with typical Indo-European nominal <i>o</i>-ablaut.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бо́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бои́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>боёв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>beating, breakage</li>
<li>battle, combat, engagement
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рукопашный.html>рукопа́шный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rukopášnyj <b>boj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">hand-to-hand <b>fight(ing)/combat</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fight, fighting, struggle</li>
<li>striking <i>(of a clock)</i></li></ol>

***бойкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бойкий.html>бо́йкий</a> (11199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bojьkъ</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бойкий.html>бо́йкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bójkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)бойче́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)бойче́й</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)бо́йче</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бойкий.html>бо́йкий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>smart, clever</li>
<li>sharp</li>
<li>glib, fluent</li>
<li>animated, busy, brisk</li></ol>

***бок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бок</a> (904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bokъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бо́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бока́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>боко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>side <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">various senses</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ná bok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sideways</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бок</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bok ó bok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">side by side</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>по́д</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бо́ком</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pód <b>bókom</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">close by</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>боку́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>bokú</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on one side</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бокал.html>бока́л</a> (3546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">boccale</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бокал.html>бока́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bokál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бокал.html>бока́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бокал.html>бока́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бокал.html>бока́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>glass, goblet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молодой.html>молоды́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выпить.html>вы́пили</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бокал.html>бока́лу</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переодеться.html>переоде́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хали</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вокзал.html>вокза́л</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Molodýje výpili po <b>bokálu</b>, pereodélisʹ i pojéxali na vokzál.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The young ones drank by the glass, changed clothes and headed off to the train station. —Tolstoy</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бокс.html>бокс</a> (6109)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бокс.html>бокс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boks</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бокс.html>бо́кса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бокс.html>бо́ксы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бокс.html>бо́ксов</a></b>)

***болван.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болван.html>болван</a> (7788)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bъlvanъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болван.html>болва́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolván</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болван.html>болва́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болван.html>болва́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болван.html>болва́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>blockhead, dimwit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">stupid person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болван.html>болва́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понять.html>по́нял</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:требоваться.html>тре́бовалось</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Étot <b>bolván</b> tak i ne pónjal štó ot nevó trébovalosʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This idiot couldn't understand what was required from him.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>dummy (in card games)</li>
<li>block <i>(for hats or wigs)</i></li></ol>

***болванка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болванка.html>болва́нка</a> (24927)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болван.html>болва́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolván</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болванка.html>болва́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolvánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болванка.html>болва́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болванка.html>болва́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болванка.html>болва́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pig, ingot, blank, block of wood, etc., serving as raw material for some product.</li>
<li>hat block, wig block, blockhead</li>
<li><i>(artillery)</i> solid projectile <i>(either armor-piercing or used as a proof shot)</i>; penetrator round; shot</li>
<li>draft outline, outline</li>
<li><i>(wiki slang)</i> stub</li>
<li><i>(office slang)</i> template, boilerplate</li>
<li>stupid woman, dummy.</li>
<li><i>(computer slang)</i> a blank CD-R /DVD-R / DVD+R <i>etc.</i> disk, or other blank optical media for burning data onto it</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bóleje</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>more
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́кий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bóleje</b> vysókij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">higher</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:менее.html>ме́нее</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bóleje</b> íli méneje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">more or less</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:полезный.html>поле́зный</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bóleje</b> poléznyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">more useful</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bóleje</b> čem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">more than</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>bóleje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">at most</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:менее.html>ме́нее</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>bóleje</b> i ne méneje, kak</i> ― <span class="e-translation">neither more nor less than, no less than</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tem <b>bóleje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">all the more, especially</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vsjó <b>bóleje</b> i <b>bóleje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">more and more</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>more than <i>(+ genitive case)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bóleje</b> vsevó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">most of all</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bóleje</b> tovó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">and what is more</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b> 20 <a href = vnd.unilang:тысяча.html>ты́сяч</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:житель.html>жи́телей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bóleje</b> 20 týsjač žítelej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">more than 20 thousand inhabitants</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>сто́ит</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>трёх</a> рубле́и</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto stóit <b>bóleje</b> trex rubléi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it costs more than three roubles</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болезнетворный.html>болезнетво́рный</a> (31271)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boléznʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:творить.html>твори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tvorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pathogenes</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a> (842)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боле́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-знь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-znʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boléznʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́зни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́зни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́зней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>disease</li>
<li>sickness, illness</li>
<li>disorder</li></ol>

***болеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боле́ть</a> (1467)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bolěti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be sick, to be ill, to be ailing
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хворать.html>хвора́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xvorátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be anxious, to be apprehensive</li>
<li>to cheer, to root for
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боле́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> спарта́к.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>boléjet</b> za Sparták.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He cheers for Spartak.</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hurt, to ache
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боли́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>bolít</b> golová.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have a headache.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">There is pain in my head.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боли́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зуб</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>bolít</b> zub.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have a toothache.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">There is pain in my tooth.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боли́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рло</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>bolít</b> górlo.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have a sore throat.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">There is pain in my throat.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боля́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>bolját</b> glazá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">My eyes hurt.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">There is pain in my eyes.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боля́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>bolját</b> nógi.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">My legs ache.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">There is pain in my legs.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***болеутоляющий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болеутоляющий.html>болеутоля́ющий</a> (27049)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1834 [see citations]. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утолять.html>утоля́ющий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">utoljájuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schmerzlindernd</i> [Arapova].
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болеутоляющий.html>болеутоля́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boleutoljájuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>analgesic, anodyne, pain-relieving</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:утолять.html>утоля́ющий</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:снимать.html>снима́ющий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боль</a><span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Мускатный <a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> мускатный <a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:содержать.html>соде́ржат</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещество.html>вещества́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стимулировать.html>стимули́руют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пищеварение.html>пищеваре́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывают</a> антибактериальное, противовоспалительное, противоотёчное, спазмолитическое <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:болеутоляющий.html>болеутоля́ющее</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствие</a>. </span></li>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:болотный.html>боло́тная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:птица.html>пти́ца</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bolótnaja</b> ptíca</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wader</span></div></dd>

***болото.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́то</a> (2510)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́то</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boloto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bolto</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">swamp; mud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бла́то</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bláto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">bláto</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">swamp; mud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">błoto</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́то</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolóto</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́та</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bog, swamp, marsh, quagmire, mire</li></ol>
